<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports selecting multiple values</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports disabled options</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports custom user input values</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports mouse, touch, and keyboard interactions</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports opening the combobox listbox with arrow keys, including automatically
focusing the first or last item accordingly</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the combobox package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> combobox</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/combobox&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>These are the key exports:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - Behavior logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> - Creates a <a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px" href="/overview/collection">collection interface</a> from an
array of items.</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to define the initial combobox value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">label</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Ghana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;gh&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">label</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Kenya&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;ke&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">//...</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<h3 id="controlled-combobox" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled combobox<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-combobox"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control the value programmatically.</p>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-input-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial input value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-input-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultInputValue</code> to prefill the input on first render.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultInputValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Nig&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlling-the-input-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling the input value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-the-input-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputValue</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInputValueChange</code> when you want to filter options as you
type.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  inputValue<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onInputValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> inputValue <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setInputValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>inputValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setOptions</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token function">filterItems</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>inputValue<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selecting-multiple-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selecting multiple values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selecting-multiple-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow selecting multiple values.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">multiple</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="using-a-custom-object-format" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using a custom object format<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-a-custom-object-format"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the combobox collection expects an array of items with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">label</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> properties. To use a custom object format, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToString</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToValue</code> properties to the collection function.</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToString</code> — A function that returns the string representation of an item.
Used to compare items when filtering.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToValue</code> — A function that returns the unique value of an item.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">itemToDisabled</code> — A function that returns the disabled state of an item.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> collection <span class="token operator">=</span> combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// custom object format</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">items</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">fruit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Banana&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">available</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">quantity</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">fruit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Apple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">available</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">quantity</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">5</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">fruit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Orange&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">available</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">quantity</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// convert item to string</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">itemToString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">fruit</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// convert item to value</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">itemToValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">id</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// convert item to disabled state</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">itemToDisabled</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">available</span> <span class="token operator">||</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">quantity</span> <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">0</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// use the collection</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="rendering-the-selected-values-outside-the-combobox" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Rendering the selected values outside the combobox<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rendering-the-selected-values-outside-the-combobox"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, selected values are shown in the input. For multiple selection, it
is often better to render selected values outside the combobox.</p>
<p>To do that:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionBehavior</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clear</code>, which clears the input value when an
item is selected.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow selecting multiple values.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Render the selected values outside the combobox.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">selectionBehavior</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;clear&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">multiple</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-the-combobox" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling the combobox<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-the-combobox"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to disable the combobox.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-an-option" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling an option<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-an-option"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isItemDisabled</code> to disable specific options.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">collection</span><span class="token operator">:</span> combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">items</span><span class="token operator">:</span> countries<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">isItemDisabled</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">      <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">disabled</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="close-on-select" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Close on select<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#close-on-select"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the menu closes when an option is selected with pointer or enter
key. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to keep it open.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnSelect</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlling-open-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling open state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code> for controlled popup state, or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code> for
an uncontrolled initial state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  open<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onOpenChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { open: boolean; reason?: string; value: string[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setOpen</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">open</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<h3 id="configuring-popup-trigger-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Configuring popup trigger behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#configuring-popup-trigger-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use these props to fine-tune when the popup opens:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnClick</code> to open when the input is clicked</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnChange</code> to control opening on input changes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnKeyPress</code> to control opening on arrow key press</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputBehavior</code> to set how typing and keyboard navigation affect
highlight/input</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">openOnClick</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">openOnChange</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">openOnKeyPress</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">inputBehavior</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;autohighlight&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>

</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="making-the-combobox-readonly" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Making the combobox readonly<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#making-the-combobox-readonly"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to make the combobox read-only.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="required-and-invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Required and invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#required-and-invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code> for form validation and UI state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
