</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-highlight-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for highlight changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-highlight-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code> to listen for highlighted option changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onHighlightChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { highlightedValue: string | null; highlightedItem: CollectionItem | null }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-initial-highlighted-option" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial highlighted option<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-highlighted-option"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultHighlightedValue</code> to set which option is highlighted when the popup
opens.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultHighlightedValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;ng&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-item-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for item selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-item-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code> to react to each selected item.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onSelect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[]; itemValue: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">itemValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to listen for selected value changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[]; items: CollectionItem[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The combobox works in forms when you:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">add a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> so the selected value is included in <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">FormData</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> to enable form submission support.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;countries&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>If the input belongs to a different form element, also set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;countries&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allowing-custom-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing custom values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-custom-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the combobox only allows values from the collection. Set
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowCustomValue</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow custom values.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowCustomValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize the trigger and clear button labels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>combobox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">triggerLabel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Open countries&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">clearTriggerLabel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Clear selection&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each combobox part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the combobox opens or closes, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> is added to content, control,
input, and trigger parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed control state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed input state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed trigger state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed content state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the combobox is focused, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is added to the control
and label parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for control focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for label focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the combobox is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the
label, control, trigger and option parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for label disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for control disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for trigger disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for item disabled state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the combobox is invalid, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute is added to the root,
label, control and input parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for root invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for label invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for control invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for input invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selected-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a combobox item is selected, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute is added to the
item part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;checked|unchecked&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for item selected state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="highlighted-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted State<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a combobox item is highlighted, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute is added
to the item part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for item highlighted state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The combobox machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the combobox</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the combobox when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state of the combobox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; label: string; control: string; input: string; content: string; trigger: string; clearTrigger: string; item: (id: string, index?: number) =&gt; string; positioner: string; itemGroup: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; itemGroupLabel: (id: string | number) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the combobox. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the combobox&#x27;s input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultInputValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the combobox&#x27;s input when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the combobox&#x27;s input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The `name` attribute of the combobox&#x27;s input. Useful for form submission</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the combobox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the combobox is disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the combobox is readonly. This puts the combobox in a &quot;non-editable&quot; mode
but the user can still interact with it</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the combobox is invalid</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the combobox is required</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">placeholder</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The placeholder text of the combobox&#x27;s input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultHighlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial highlighted value of the combobox when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the highlighted value of the combobox.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled highlighted value of the combobox</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the combobox&#x27;s selected items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the combobox&#x27;s selected items when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the combobox&#x27;s selected items.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputBehavior</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;autohighlight&quot; | &quot;autocomplete&quot; | &quot;none&quot;</code><span class="d_block">Defines the auto-completion behavior of the combobox.

- `autohighlight`: The first focused item is highlighted as the user types
- `autocomplete`: Navigating the listbox with the arrow keys selects the item and the input is updated</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionBehavior</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;clear&quot; | &quot;replace&quot; | &quot;preserve&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The behavior of the combobox input when an item is selected

- `replace`: The selected item string is set as the input value
- `clear`: The input value is cleared
- `preserve`: The input value is preserved</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to autofocus the input on mount</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnClick</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to open the combobox popup on initial click on the input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean | ((details: InputValueChangeDetails) =&gt; boolean)</code><span class="d_block">Whether to show the combobox when the input value changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowCustomValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow typing custom values in the input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alwaysSubmitOnEnter</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to always submit on Enter key press, even if popup is open.
Useful for single-field autocomplete forms where Enter should submit the form.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to loop the keyboard navigation through the items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">positioning</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">PositioningOptions</code><span class="d_block">The positioning options to dynamically position the menu</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInputValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: InputValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the input&#x27;s value changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when a new item is selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: HighlightChangeDetails&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an item is highlighted using the pointer
or keyboard navigation.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: SelectionDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an item is selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onOpenChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: OpenChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the popup is opened</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">ListCollection&lt;T&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The collection of items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow multiple selection.

**Good to know:** When `multiple` is `true`, the `selectionBehavior` is automatically set to `clear`.
It is recommended to render the selected items in a separate container.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to close the combobox when an item is selected.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">openOnKeyPress</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to open the combobox on arrow key press</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToIndexFn</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ScrollToIndexDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to scroll to a specific index</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">composite</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the combobox is a composed with other composite widgets like tabs</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disableLayer</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to disable registering this a dismissable layer</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">navigate</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: NavigateDetails) =&gt; ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--transform-origin</kbd></div><span>The transform origin for animations</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Content</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--layer-index</kbd></div><span>The index of the dismissable in the layer stack</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Backdrop</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div bdr_3px">--layer-index</kbd></div><span>The index of the dismissable in the layer stack</span></div></div></div></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/combobox/" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Combobox WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>When the combobox is closed, opens the listbox and highlights to the first option.
When the combobox is open, moves focus to the next option.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>When the combobox is closed, opens the listbox and highlights to the last option.
When the combobox is open, moves focus to the previous option.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Home</kbd></div><div>When the combobox is open, moves focus to the first option.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">End</kbd></div><div>When the combobox is open, moves focus to the last option.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Escape</kbd></div><div>Closes the listbox.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div>Selects the highlighted option and closes the combobox.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Esc</kbd></div><div>Closes the combobox</div></li></ul><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/components/combobox.mdx" class="d_inline-flex ai_center gap_1 \"@zag-js/combobox\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the key exports:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - Behavior - Creates a \u003ca href=\"/overview/collection\"\u003ecollection interface\u003c/a\u003e from an\narray of items.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"combobox/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e to define the initial combobox value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{13}\"\u003econst collection = combobox.collection({\n  items: [\n    { label: \"Nigeria\", value: \"ng\" },\n    { label: \"Ghana\", value: \"gh\" },\n    { label: \"Kenya\", value: \"ke\" },\n    //...\n  ],\n})\n\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultValue: [\"ng\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled combobox\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to control the value programmatically.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"combobox/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial input value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003edefaultInputValue\u003c/code\u003e to prefill the input on first render.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultInputValue: \"Nig\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling the input value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003einputValue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonInputValueChange\u003c/code\u003e when you want to filter options as you\ntype.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  inputValue,\n  onInputValueChange({ inputValue }) {\n    setInputValue(inputValue)\n    setOptions(filterItems(inputValue))\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelecting multiple values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to allow selecting multiple values.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  multiple: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing a custom object format\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the combobox collection expects an array of items with \u003ccode\u003elabel\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e properties. To use a custom object format, pass the \u003ccode\u003eitemToString\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003eitemToValue\u003c/code\u003e properties to the collection function.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToString\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the string representation of an item.\nUsed to compare items when filtering.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToValue\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the unique value of an item.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eitemToDisabled\u003c/code\u003e — A function that returns the disabled state of an item.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst collection = combobox.collection({\n  // custom object format\n  items: [\n    { id: 1, fruit: \"Banana\", available: true, quantity: 10 },\n    { id: 2, fruit: \"Apple\", available: false, quantity: 5 },\n    { id: 3, fruit: \"Orange\", available: true, quantity: 3 },\n    //...\n  ],\n  // convert item to string\n  itemToString(item) {\n    return item.fruit\n  },\n  // convert item to value\n  itemToValue(item) {\n    return item.id\n  },\n  // convert item to disabled state\n  itemToDisabled(item) {\n    return !item.available || item.quantity === 0\n  },\n})\n\n// use the collection\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRendering the selected values outside the combobox\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, selected values are shown in the input. For multiple selection, it\nis often better to render selected values outside the combobox.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo do that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSet the \u003ccode\u003eselectionBehavior\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003eclear\u003c/code\u003e, which clears the input value when an\nitem is selected.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSet the \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e property to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to allow selecting multiple values.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRender the selected values outside the combobox.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  selectionBehavior: \"clear\",\n  multiple: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling the combobox\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edisabled\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to disable the combobox.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling an option\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass \u003ccode\u003eisItemDisabled\u003c/code\u003e to disable specific options.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{6-8}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection: combobox.collection({\n    items: countries,\n    isItemDisabled(item) {\n      return item.disabled\n    },\n  }),\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClose on select\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the menu closes when an option is selected with pointer or enter\nkey. Set \u003ccode\u003ecloseOnSelect\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to keep it open.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling open \u003ccode\u003edefaultOpen\u003c/code\u003e for\nan uncontrolled initial state.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean; reason?: string; value: string[] }\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eConfiguring popup trigger behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse these props to fine-tune when the popup opens:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eopenOnClick\u003c/code\u003e to open when the input is you can target in CSS.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eOpen and closed state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the combobox opens or closes, \u003ccode\u003edata-state\u003c/code\u003e is added to content, control,\ninput, and trigger parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"control\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFocused State\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the combobox is focused, the \u003ccode\u003edata-focus\u003c/code\u003e attribute is added to likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T2de2,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A combobox is an input with a popup that lets you select a value from a\ncollection.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/combobox\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Combobox\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports selecting multiple values\n- Supports disabled options\n- Supports custom user input values\n- Supports mouse, touch, and keyboard interactions\n- Supports opening the combobox listbox with arrow keys, including automatically\n  focusing the first or last item accordingly\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the combobox package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"combobox/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the combobox anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"combobox\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the combobox package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as combobox from \"@zag-js/combobox\"\n```\n\nThese are the key exports:\n\n- `machine` - Behavior logic.\n- `connect` - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\n- `collection` - Creates a [collection interface](/overview/collection) from an\n  array of items.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"combobox/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nSet `defaultValue` to define the initial combobox value.\n\n```jsx {13}\nconst collection = combobox.collection({\n  items: [\n    { label: \"Nigeria\", value: \"ng\" },\n    { label: \"Ghana\", value: \"gh\" },\n    { label: \"Kenya\", value: \"ke\" },\n    //...\n  ],\n})\n\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultValue: [\"ng\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled combobox\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control the value programmatically.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"combobox/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial input value\n\nUse `defaultInputValue` to prefill the input on first render.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultInputValue: \"Nig\",\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling the input value\n\nUse `inputValue` and `onInputValueChange` when you want to filter options as you\ntype.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  inputValue,\n  onInputValueChange({ inputValue }) {\n    setInputValue(inputValue)\n    setOptions(filterItems(inputValue))\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Selecting multiple values\n\nSet `multiple` to `true` to allow selecting multiple values.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  multiple: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Using a custom object format\n\nBy default, the combobox collection expects an array of items with `label` and\n`value` properties. To use a custom object format, pass the `itemToString` and\n`itemToValue` properties to the collection function.\n\n- `itemToString` — A function that returns the string representation of an item.\n  Used to compare items when filtering.\n- `itemToValue` — A function that returns the unique value of an item.\n- `itemToDisabled` — A function that returns the disabled state of an item.\n\n```jsx\nconst collection = combobox.collection({\n  // custom object format\n  items: [\n    { id: 1, fruit: \"Banana\", available: true, quantity: 10 },\n    { id: 2, fruit: \"Apple\", available: false, quantity: 5 },\n    { id: 3, fruit: \"Orange\", available: true, quantity: 3 },\n    //...\n  ],\n  // convert item to string\n  itemToString(item) {\n    return item.fruit\n  },\n  // convert item to value\n  itemToValue(item) {\n    return item.id\n  },\n  // convert item to disabled state\n  itemToDisabled(item) {\n    return !item.available || item.quantity === 0\n  },\n})\n\n// use the collection\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n})\n```\n\n### Rendering the selected values outside the combobox\n\nBy default, selected values are shown in the input. For multiple selection, it\nis often better to render selected values outside the combobox.\n\nTo do that:\n\n- Set the `selectionBehavior` to `clear`, which clears the input value when an\n  item is selected.\n- Set the `multiple` property to `true` to allow selecting multiple values.\n- Render the selected values outside the combobox.\n\n```jsx {4-6}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  selectionBehavior: \"clear\",\n  multiple: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling the combobox\n\nSet `disabled` to `true` to disable the combobox.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling an option\n\nPass `isItemDisabled` to disable specific options.\n\n```jsx {6-8}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection: combobox.collection({\n    items: countries,\n    isItemDisabled(item) {\n      return item.disabled\n    },\n  }),\n})\n```\n\n### Close on select\n\nBy default, the menu closes when an option is selected with pointer or enter\nkey. Set `closeOnSelect` to `false` to keep it open.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling open state\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` for controlled popup state, or `defaultOpen` for\nan uncontrolled initial state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  open,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean; reason?: string; value: string[] }\n    setOpen(details.open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Configuring popup trigger behavior\n\nUse these props to fine-tune when the popup opens:\n\n- `openOnClick` to open when the input is clicked\n- `openOnChange` to control opening on input changes\n- `openOnKeyPress` to control opening on arrow key press\n- `inputBehavior` to set how typing and keyboard navigation affect\n  highlight/input\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  openOnClick: true,\n  openOnChange: false,\n  openOnKeyPress: false,\n  inputBehavior: \"autohighlight\",\n})\n```\n\n### Positioning the popup\n\nUse `positioning` to control how the popup is placed.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  positioning: { placement: \"bottom-start\" },\n})\n```\n\n### Submitting forms on Enter\n\nSet `alwaysSubmitOnEnter` to `true` if you want Enter to submit the form even\nwhile the popup is open.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  alwaysSubmitOnEnter: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Making the combobox readonly\n\nSet `readOnly` to `true` to make the combobox read-only.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  readOnly: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Required and invalid state\n\nSet `required` and `invalid` for form validation and UI state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  required: true,\n  invalid: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for highlight changes\n\nUse `onHighlightChange` to listen for highlighted option changes.\n\n```jsx {3-6}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null; highlightedItem: CollectionItem | null }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the initial highlighted option\n\nUse `defaultHighlightedValue` to set which option is highlighted when the popup\nopens.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultHighlightedValue: \"ng\",\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for item selection\n\nUse `onSelect` to react to each selected item.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onSelect(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[]; itemValue: string }\n    console.log(details.itemValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value changes\n\nUse `onValueChange` to listen for selected value changes.\n\n```jsx {3-6}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[]; items: CollectionItem[] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nThe combobox works in forms when you:\n\n- add a `name` so the selected value is included in `FormData`.\n\nSet `name` to enable form submission support.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  name: \"countries\",\n})\n```\n\nIf the input belongs to a different form element, also set `form`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  name: \"countries\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n### Allowing custom values\n\nBy default, the combobox only allows values from the collection. Set\n`allowCustomValue` to `true` to allow custom values.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  allowCustomValue: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility labels\n\nUse `translations` to customize the trigger and clear button labels.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(combobox.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  translations: {\n    triggerLabel: \"Open countries\",\n    clearTriggerLabel: \"Clear selection\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach combobox part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nWhen the combobox opens or closes, `data-state` is added to content, control,\ninput, and trigger parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed control state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed input state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed trigger state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed content state */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused State\n\nWhen the combobox is focused, the `data-focus` attribute is added to the control\nand label parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for control focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for label focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled State\n\nWhen the combobox is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is added to the\nlabel, control, trigger and option parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for label disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for control disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for trigger disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for item disabled state */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid State\n\nWhen the combobox is invalid, the `data-invalid` attribute is added to the root,\nlabel, control and input parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for root invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for label invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for control invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for input invalid state */\n}\n```\n\n### Selected State\n\nWhen a combobox item is selected, the `data-state` attribute is added to the\nitem part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for item selected state */\n}\n```\n\n### Highlighted State\n\nWhen a combobox item is highlighted, the `data-highlighted` attribute is added\nto the item part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for item highlighted state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe combobox machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"combobox\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe combobox `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"combobox\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"combobox\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"combobox\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[Combobox WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/combobox/).\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"combobox\"
